 vah manovigyaan kii chaatra he or usne police ke saamne apana gunaah kabool kar liya he

 police aaropee ladki ke doston or parijanon se poochtacha kar rahi he

 ye ek aisa chalange he, jisamen aapako group admin dwaara die gaye kai task ko 50 dinon ke andar puraa karnaa hota he

 task puraa karne ke baad aakhri main jo image ubhartee he, wo whale machhlee kii tarah hoti he
 This game is a game of death
 After signing in this game, you get the challenge to complete the task within 50 days
 isamen khud ko nuksaan pahunchaana, akele main daraavnee filmein dekhnaa or whale machhlee kaa aakaar apane haath par godana jaisi chunautiyaan shaamil hai
 The most dreadful and last task of this game is given on the 50th day, in which the challenge is to kill oneself
 haath par blade se likhte hai code F57is game kaa admin skip ke jariye game khilne vaale se lagaataar sampark main rahata he
 The game player is given a code number every day
 isamen haath par blade se F57 likhakar isaki photo aplod karne ke liye kaha jaataa he
 The winner of the game is declared as the one who dies on the 50th
 ab tak 130 logon kii mautmasoom bachche game samajhakar iske jaal main funs rahe hai

 yah apradhi kism ke logon kaa ek trep he

 iske baavjood aseem ne apane khilaaf lage deshadroh ke aaropon ko hataae jane tak jail se baahar aane se inkaar kar diya
 Meanwhile, India Against Corruption (IAC) activist Arvind Kejriwal warned that if Aseem is not released, he will sit on a sit-in protest outside the jail
 isi bich maharashtra nav nirmaan sena ke pramukh raaj thakare ne bhi uttar pradesh ke nivasee aseem kaa samarthan kiya he
 a division bench of Chief Justice Mohit Shah and Justice Nitin Jamadar granted bail to Asim while hearing a PIL filed by advocate Sanskar Marathi
 india against karpshan (iasi) kii kaaryakarta priti menon ne bataaya ki paanch hajaar rupee ke muchalke par aseem ko jamaanat mili
 Mayank Gandhi of the IAC said that Aseem has refused to come out of jail till the withdrawal of the sedition charges leveled against him by the Mumbai Police
 grahamantri aaraar patil ne kaha tha ki police evam kanoon vibhaag se aseem ke khilaaf lagaae gaye deshadroh ke aarope par raay maangi jaaegi
 Hours later, the cartoonist refused to come out of prison
 kejariwal ne isse pehle kaha tha, "aseem ko reeha karo yaa hamen giraftaar karo
 "he said," Aseem has fought against corruption and for the Lokpal but has been termed as a traitor and those who have stolen coal are being called patriots
 " Kejriwal said Patil, Information and Broadcasting Minister Ambika Soni and Congress spokesperson Manish Tiwari have accepted that a suitable case was not made against Trivedi
 patil ne isse pehle sweekaar kiya tha ki trivedi ke khilaaf maamle main grih mantralay kii koi bhoomika nahin thi or saath hi unhone aashwaasan diya tha ki vah unki jald rihaai kii koshish karenge
 Raj demanded withdrawal of treason case against Aseem and release him
 ek cartoonist ke rup main raaj ne kaha ki aseem ne keval cartoon ke dwaara apane gusse ko baahar nikaala he

 " raaj ne prashn kiya ki kyon afjal guru evam ajmal kasaab ko faansee dene main deree kii jaati he or cartoonist ko deshadroh kaa saamana karnaa padataa he
 The 25-year-old Trivedi, who is associated with the anti-corruption campaign of Anna Hazare, is accused of putting 'hateful and objectionable' material on his website and putting up a banner insulting the Constitution during the anti-corruption Anna Hazare movement in December last year
 tippaniyan He was arrested from bandra-kurla after the police issued a non-bailable warrant against him
 bandra ke magistrate ne unhen ravivaar ko saat din kii police hiraasat main bheja tha
